3:17 The biggest reason why some people succeed while other people fail. Full uncut Minecraft let's plays are only viable as livestreams because of the excitement of it being live. When it's a pre-recorded video, you should definitely cut out the boring parts and only leave in the fun parts. My brother livestreamed and uploaded them uncut to YouTube. He got nowhere after 2 years and quit. I'm also not very good with YouTube because of the crappy games that I play. Funny relatively short edited let's play videos with just the best moments are way more worth a watch than a mostly boring 2 hour let's play video. The problem is that most people are too lazy to edit their videos or don't have enough time because they spend 8 or even 12 hours at work and are also exhausted. I have no excuse. I have enough time and money. I have to start doing something with my life NOW.
